<td>阿贝尔群
</td>
<td>阿贝尔群（<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {Z} _{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">Z</mi>
</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {Z} _{2}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \mathbb {Z} _{2}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/92aedfb5c02eff978ab963421ce930f46801657e" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.605ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>）
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%8A%E7%BE%A4" title="半群">半群</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%93%AC%E7%BE%A4" title="拟群">拟群</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%BA%E5%8D%8A%E7%BE%A4" title="幺半群">幺半群</a>是类似于群的结构，但更具一般性。它们由一个集合和一个封闭二元运算所组成，但不必然满足其他条件。<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%8A%E7%BE%A4" title="半群">半群</a>有一<i>结合</i>二元运算，但没有单位元素。<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%BA%E5%8D%8A%E7%BE%A4" title="幺半群">幺半群</a>是一有单位元素但可能没有每个元素之逆元素的半群。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%93%AC%E7%BE%A4" title="拟群">拟群</a>满足任一元素皆以一唯一的前或后运算转换成另一元素，但此一二元运算可能不具结合律。
</p><p>所有的群都是幺半群，且所有的幺半群都是半群。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.92.B0.E5.92.8C.E9.AB.94.EF.BC.8D.E5.85.B7.E5.85.A9.E5.80.8B.E4.BA.8C.E5.85.83.E9.81.8B.E7.AE.97.E7.9A.84.E7.B5.90.E6.A7.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="环和体－具两个二元运算的结构">环和体－具两个二元运算的结构</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：环和体－具两个二元运算的结构">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E7%8E%AF_(%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B0)" title="环 (代数)">环 (代数)</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9F%9F_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8)" title="域 (数学)">域 (数学)</a></div> <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">参见：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%92%B0%E8%AB%96" title="环论">环论</a>、<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%92%B0%E8%AB%96%E8%A9%9E%E5%BD%99%E8%A1%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="环论词汇表（页面不存在）">环论词汇表</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%AB%94%E8%AB%96" title="体论">体论</a>和<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%AB%94%E8%AB%96%E8%A9%9E%E5%BD%99%E8%A1%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="体论词汇表（页面不存在）">体论词汇表</a></div>
<p>群只有一个二元运算。但为了完整说明不同类型的数之行为，具两个运算子的结构是需要的。其中最重要的为<a href="/wiki/%E7%8E%AF_(%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B0)" title="环 (代数)">环</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9F%9F_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8)" title="域 (数学)">体</a>。
</p><p><b><a href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E9%85%8D%E5%BE%8B" title="分配律">分配律</a></b>广义化了数中的<i>分配律</i>，且要求其运算子运算时应采之顺序（称为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%81%8B%E7%AE%97%E9%A0%86%E5%BA%8F" title="运算顺序">优先权</a>）。对于整数而言，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (a+b)\times c=a\times c+b\times c}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>b</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<mi>c</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<mi>c</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>b</mi>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<mi>c</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (a+b)\times c=a\times c+b\times c}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle (a+b)\times c=a\times c+b\times c}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f17a22f7efbc086d3f4bc4a0d98457b25b9b89c3" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:26.585ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle c\times (a+b)=c\times a+c\times b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mi>c</mi>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>b</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>c</mi>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>c</mi>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<mi>b</mi>

</semantics>

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \times }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\times" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0ffafff1ad26cbe49045f19a67ce532116a32703" style="vertical-align: 0.019ex; margin-bottom: -0.19ex; width:1.808ex; height:1.509ex;"/></span>称之此于+上是<i>可分配</i>的。
</p><p><b><a href="/wiki/%E7%8E%AF_(%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B0)" title="环 (代数)">环</a></b>有两个二元运算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle +}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>+</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle +}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="+" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/fe6ef363cd19902d1a7a71fb1c8b21e8ede52406" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:1.808ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \times }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \times }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \times }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0ffafff1ad26cbe49045f19a67ce532116a32703" style="vertical-align: 0.019ex; margin-bottom: -0.19ex; width:1.808ex; height:1.509ex;"/></span>，其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \times }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \times }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\times" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0ffafff1ad26cbe49045f19a67ce532116a32703" style="vertical-align: 0.019ex; margin-bottom: -0.19ex; width:1.808ex; height:1.509ex;"/></span>于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle +}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>+</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle +}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="+" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/fe6ef363cd19902d1a7a71fb1c8b21e8ede52406" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:1.808ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>上是可分配的。在第一个运算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle +}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>+</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle +}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="+" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/fe6ef363cd19902d1a7a71fb1c8b21e8ede52406" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:1.808ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>下，它会形成一个<i>阿贝尔群</i>。而在第二个运算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \times }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \times }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \times }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0ffafff1ad26cbe49045f19a67ce532116a32703" style="vertical-align: 0.019ex; margin-bottom: -0.19ex; width:1.808ex; height:1.509ex;"/></span>下，其为结合的，但不需要有一单位元素或逆元素，所以除法是不被允许的。其加法<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle +}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>+</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle +}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="+" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/fe6ef363cd19902d1a7a71fb1c8b21e8ede52406" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:1.808ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>单位元写成<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2aae8864a3c1fec9585261791a809ddec1489950" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.162ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，而其<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的加法逆元则写成<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle -a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle -a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="-a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6e0982b5868a66be1ed3ad7ef4bcd3d3db20f982" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:3.038ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>。
</p><p>整数是环的一个例子。其有使其为一<b><a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B4%E7%8E%AF" title="整环">整环</a></b>的额外性质。
</p><p><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9F%9F_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8)" title="域 (数学)">体</a></b>是一具有在运算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \times }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \times }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \times }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0ffafff1ad26cbe49045f19a67ce532116a32703" style="vertical-align: 0.019ex; margin-bottom: -0.19ex; width:1.808ex; height:1.509ex;"/></span>下，除了<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2aae8864a3c1fec9585261791a809ddec1489950" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.162ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的所有元素会形成一<i>阿贝尔群</i>之额外性质的环。其乘法<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \times }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \times }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \times }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0ffafff1ad26cbe49045f19a67ce532116a32703" style="vertical-align: 0.019ex; margin-bottom: -0.19ex; width:1.808ex; height:1.509ex;"/></span>单位元素写成<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/92d98b82a3778f043108d4e20960a9193df57cbf" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.162ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，而其<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的乘法逆元则写成<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{-1}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{-1}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a^{{-1}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3f5709c8d86f7fec8fb86069bf5d15a9eabe564e" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.563ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>。
</p><p>有理数、实数和复数都是体的例子。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E4.BB.A3.E6.95.B8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="代数">代数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：代数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><b>代数</b>一词亦可用来称呼不同的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8%E7%B5%90%E6%A7%8B" title="代数结构">代数结构</a>，包含有：
</p>
<ul><li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A4%E6%8F%9B%E7%92%B0%E4%B8%8A%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8" title="交换环上的代数">交换环上的代数</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88%E4%B8%8A%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8" title="集合上的代数">集合上的代数</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%83%E5%B0%94%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B0" title="布尔代数">布尔代数</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%AF%84%E7%96%87%E8%AB%96" title="范畴论">范畴论</a>内的<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=F-%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="F-代数（页面不存在）">F-代数</a>和<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=F-%E5%B0%8D%E5%81%B6%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="F-对偶代数（页面不存在）">F-对偶代数</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%CE%A3%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8" title="Σ代数">Σ代数</a></li></ul>
